\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__mdc__interface_8h_a2a841ce582ce97f62df6334717b49fcb}{}\label{le__mdc__interface_8h_a2a841ce582ce97f62df6334717b49fcb}
Connect the current client thread to the service providing this A\+PI. Block until the service is available.

For each thread that wants to use this A\+PI, either Connect\+Service or Try\+Connect\+Service must be called before any other functions in this A\+PI. Normally, Connect\+Service is automatically called for the main thread, but not for any other thread. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function is created automatically. \index{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Disconnect\+Service@{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Disconnect\+Service}}
\index{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Disconnect\+Service@{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Disconnect\+Service}!le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Disconnect\+Service(void)}{le_mdc_DisconnectService(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Disconnect\+Service (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__mdc__interface_8h_a3ce7efc114de8b91a7ad61cb6f6f47c8}{}\label{le__mdc__interface_8h_a3ce7efc114de8b91a7ad61cb6f6f47c8}
Disconnect the current client thread from the service providing this A\+PI.

Normally, this function doesn\textquotesingle{}t need to be called. After this function is called, there\textquotesingle{}s no longer a connection to the service, and the functions in this A\+PI can\textquotesingle{}t be used. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function is created automatically. \index{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Get\+A\+PN@{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Get\+A\+PN}}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+OW if the IP address can\textquotesingle{}t fit in buffer

\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

Set the Access Point Name (A\+PN) for the given profile.

The A\+PN must be an A\+S\+C\+II string.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER if an input parameter is not valid
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT if the data session is currently connected for the given profile
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If A\+PN is too long (max A\+P\+N\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+L\+EN digits), it is a fatal error, the function will not return.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The maximum A\+PN length might be limited by the platform. Please refer to the platform documentation \hyperlink{platformConstraintsMdc}{Modem Control platform constraints}.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The process exits, if an invalid profile object is given 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em profile\+Ref} & Query this profile object \\
\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Set\+Authentication(le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Profile\+Ref\+\_\+t profile\+Ref, le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Auth\+\_\+t type, const char $\ast$\+L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+N\+U\+L\+L user\+Name, const char $\ast$\+L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+N\+U\+L\+L password)}{le_mdc_SetAuthentication(le_mdc_ProfileRef_t profileRef, le_mdc_Auth_t type, const char *LE_NONNULL userName, const char *LE_NONNULL password)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Set\+Authentication (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Profile\+Ref\+\_\+t}}]{profile\+Ref, }
\item[{{\bf le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Auth\+\_\+t}}]{type, }
\item[{const char $\ast$L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+N\+U\+LL}]{user\+Name, }
\item[{const char $\ast$L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+N\+U\+LL}]{password}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__mdc__interface_8h_a9f69d0751927b5ead6c756202179b222}{}\label{le__mdc__interface_8h_a9f69d0751927b5ead6c756202179b222}
Set authentication property

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK on success
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The process exits, if user\+Name or password are N\+U\+LL when type is not P\+A\+\_\+\+M\+D\+C\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+H\+\_\+\+N\+O\+NE
\item The process exits, if an invalid profile object is given 
\end{DoxyItemize}

If user\+Name is too long (max U\+S\+E\+R\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+L\+EN digits), it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 

If password is too long (max P\+A\+S\+S\+W\+O\+R\+D\+\_\+\+N\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+L\+EN digits), it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 

Both P\+AP and C\+H\+AP authentication can be set for 3\+G\+PP network\+: in this case, the device decides which authentication procedure is performed. For example, the device can have a policy to select the most secure authentication mechanism. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service}}
\index{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service}!le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service(void)}{le_mdc_TryConnectService(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+mdc\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__mdc__interface_8h_ac93bebcbe5364e7313a168e9502c30b6}{}\label{le__mdc__interface_8h_ac93bebcbe5364e7313a168e9502c30b6}
Try to connect the current client thread to the service providing this A\+PI. Return with an error if the service is not available.

For each thread that wants to use this A\+PI, either Connect\+Service or Try\+Connect\+Service must be called before any other functions in this A\+PI. Normally, Connect\+Service is automatically called for the main thread, but not for any other thread. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function is created automatically.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK if the client connected successfully to the service.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+A\+V\+A\+I\+L\+A\+B\+LE if the server is not currently offering the service to which the client is bound.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+M\+I\+T\+T\+ED if the client interface is not bound to any service (doesn\textquotesingle{}t have a binding).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+M\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR if the Service Directory cannot be reached. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
